-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `cache`
--

CREATE TABLE `cache` (
  `name` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `result` mediumtext NOT NULL,
  `tarih` datetime NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin5;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `config`
--

CREATE TABLE `config` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `ckey` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_turkish_ci NOT NULL,
  `cvalue` text CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_turkish_ci NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `epostalog`
--

CREATE TABLE `epostalog` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `from` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `to` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `body` text NOT NULL,
  `IP` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `tarih` datetime NOT NULL,
  `randStr` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `durum` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin5;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `esantiyon`
--

CREATE TABLE `esantiyon` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `urunler` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `kategoriler` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `tanim` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `indirimOran` double NOT NULL,
  `maxAdet` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `filitre`
--

CREATE TABLE `filitre` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `baslik` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_turkish_ci NOT NULL,
  `icerik` text CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_turkish_ci NOT NULL,
  `seq` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `filitredetay`
--

CREATE TABLE `filitredetay` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `baslik` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `icerik` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `firmalar`
--

CREATE TABLE `firmalar` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(256) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin5;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `fiyatbirim`
--

CREATE TABLE `fiyatbirim` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `code` varchar(8) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `value` double NOT NULL,
  `data1` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data2` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data3` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `iletisim`
--

CREATE TABLE `iletisim` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `urunID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `namelastname` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `ceptel` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `subject` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `message` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `answer` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data1` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data2` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data3` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data4` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data5` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `tarih` datetime NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `iletisimcevap`

  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin5;

  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,

  `startDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `finishDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `puan` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `kombine`
--

CREATE TABLE `kombine` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `tanim` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `marka` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `kategori` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `urun` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `indirim` double NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_general_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `lang`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `lang`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `lang` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `key` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `code` varchar(8) NOT NULL,
  `value` text NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin5;

  `data1` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data2` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data3` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data4` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data5` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data6` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data7` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data8` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data9` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data` longtext CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `code` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `seolinks`
--

CREATE TABLE `seolinks` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `key` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `urun` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `kategori` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `ktype` smallint(6) NOT NULL,
  `redirect` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `from` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `body` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `tarih` datetime NOT NULL,
  `seq` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `teslimat`
--

CREATE TABLE `teslimat` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `degisimYuzde` double NOT NULL,
  `degisimYTL` double NOT NULL,
  `seq` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `topluindirim`
--

CREATE TABLE `topluindirim` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `baslik` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `kategori` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `marka` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `filitre` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `indirimOran` double NOT NULL,
  `start` datetime NOT NULL,
  `finish` datetime NOT NULL,
  `mail` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `urun` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

  `detay` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_turkish_ci NOT NULL,
  `resim` varchar(512) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim2` varchar(512) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim3` varchar(512) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,

  `resim8` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `resim9` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `resim10` varchar(128) NOT NULL,

  `download2` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `download3` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,

  `download5` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,

  `urunBirim` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `fiyatBirim` varchar(16) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `fiyat` double NOT NULL,

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `urunpaket`
--

CREATE TABLE `urunpaket` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `urunIDs` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `amount` double NOT NULL,
  `percent` double NOT NULL,
  `birim` varchar(16) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin5;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `urunvar`
--

CREATE TABLE `urunvar` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `urunID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `varID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `varName` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim1` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim2` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim3` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim4` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `resim5` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `data` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `urunvars`
--

CREATE TABLE `urunvars` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `urunID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `varID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `var` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `fark` double NOT NULL,
  `up` tinyint(1) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `urunvarstok`
--

CREATE TABLE `urunvarstok` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `urunID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `var1` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `var2` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `kod` varchar(16) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `stok` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `fark` double NOT NULL,
  `up` tinyint(1) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `urunXML`
--

CREATE TABLE `urunXML` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `penta` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `indexKatalog` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `indexFiyat` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `indexStok` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `parentID` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin5;

-- Tablo döküm verisi `urunXML`
--

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `urunYorum`
--

CREATE TABLE `urunYorum` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `userID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `urunID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `puan` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sitePuan` double NOT NULL,
  `aciklama` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `tarih` date NOT NULL,
  `onay` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `detay` text CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `tip` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tablo için tablo yapısı `user`
--

CREATE TABLE `user` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `facebookID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `resim` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `lastname` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `birthdate` date NOT NULL,
  `sex` varchar(16) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `semt` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `username` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `address` varchar(512) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
  `city` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET latin5 NOT NULL,
